## 1. Executive Summary

### 1.1 Project Overview

**ReliefSync** is a comprehensive disaster relief management platform designed to coordinate emergency response between multiple stakeholders: citizens, NGOs, government agencies, and field agents. The platform leverages modern web technologies, AI/ML capabilities, and real-time communication to provide efficient disaster management.

## 2. Project Vision & Goals

### 2.1 Vision Statement

> *"To create a unified, intelligent disaster relief platform that saves lives through faster response times, efficient resource allocation, and seamless coordination between all stakeholders."*

## 8. Phase 5: Backend Development

â”‚  â”‚  â”‚    socket.on('new-disaster', (data) => {                    â”‚   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  â”‚      io.to('admin').emit('disaster-alert', data);           â”‚   â”‚   â”‚
